### Round 6: Monaco Grand Prix
*Date: 2011-05-29*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 8: European Grand Prix
*Date: 2011-06-26*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
